# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
#saal ^4kQG4nJZ

have n jobs, V runs for wᵢ seconds. we have a resource that can be used for W seconds. V job finished we get 0.01*wᵢ reward ^6RXmsENx

goal ^hLEPvZGe

maximize reward ^b8PZrUHZ

example ^kcp572Fd

Oᵢ ^roW2UZV7

OPT(i) ^TxB2YP6X

solution ^ScMdchgC

lemma ^iGiUFzEu

if i ne Oᵢ ⟶ OPT(i)=OPT(i-1)  ^hMWf1vhh

if i e Oᵢ nE expression ∴ we add a variable (enlarge solution space) ^hX8hewmb

keep track of total time ^Z944hvO4

if we schedule interval i, W-wᵢ seconds remain ^J5jQiuzA

subproblem ^WAQMqbMv

w. V seconds and i, what is optimal value I possible w. 1, 2,..., i jobs ^j3KEDIBJ

I=OPT(i,V) ^Htdm6iqy

if i ne Oᵢv ^eyywn9z2

if i e Oᵢv ^hv2XVMBo

OPT(i,V)=OPT(i-1,V) ^Xn8bjboD

OPT(i,V)=wᵢ+OPT(i-1,V-wᵢ) ^vVU5mIMM

main theorem ^dU9pR2OM

OPT(0,V)=0 foreach V>=0 ^RpJhbhr6

if i>=1 ^cqQFoYlT

V<wᵢ ⟶ OPT(i,V)=OPT(i-1,V) ^r6VTWeuQ

V>=wᵢ ⟶ OPT(i,V)=max(OPT(i-1,V), wᵢ+OPT(i-1,V-wᵢ))  ^on7aV49j

yields a 2D table ^NqjqETz1

optimal solution ^NyTV40UV

algorithm ^svnlJs8U

fills up table ^ydXlhuYI

using ^LgG2MrSI

runtime ^9xbMdnlw

O(nW) ^QuyIHhfX

only polymomial ^lKrmoogb

W polynomial related to n (W=2n for example) ^n49Ig9On

dynamic programming ^M8t7lqyY

NP-hard = NP-complete ^1TTTeahr
